    <div class="container home-page__container">
     <script>
      function doSearch() {
      var queryterm = $j("input#coveodesktopsearchinput").val();
      if (queryterm === "")
        queryterm = $j("input#coveomobilesearchinput").val();
      if (queryterm === "") return;
      var u = '/search#q=' + queryterm + '&sort=relevancy';
      if (window.location.host.split('.')[0].match("cme") != null)
        u += "&f:coveoContentTypeFacet=[CME]";
      window.location.replace(u);
    }

    $j(document).ready(function () {
      $j('#coveodesktopsearchinput,#coveomobilesearchinput').bind('keypress keydown keyup', function (e) {
        if (e.keyCode === 13 && $j(this).val()) {
          e.preventDefault();
          doSearch();
        }
      });
    });
     </script>

          <h2 class="card-title">
           <a href="/news/endocrinology/20210321/genetic-data-show-evidence-for-male-pcos-with-cardiometabolic-consequences">
            Genetic data show evidence for male PCOS, with cardiometabolic consequences
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="card-body">
           <a class="article-mug" href="/news/endocrinology/20210321/genetic-data-show-evidence-for-male-pcos-with-cardiometabolic-consequences">
            <img alt="Genetic data show evidence for &amp;lsquo;male PCOS,&amp;rsquo; with cardiometabolic consequences" class="article-listing-img" onerror="this.style.display='none'" onload="requestMasonryReflow()" src="/~/media/slack-news/endocrinology/mugs/z/zhu_jia_2021_web.jpg?w=80"/>
           </a>
           <p class="card-text">
            Genetic risk factors for polycystic ovary syndrome can act independently of ovarian function, causing cardiometabolic dysfunction and hyperandrogenism through biological pathways common to both men and women, according to a speaker.
           </p>

       <script>
        var reflowTimer;
  function requestMasonryReflow() {
    console.log("Masonry: Reflow requested.");
    if (!$('.card--layout').data('masonry')) {
      console.log("Masonry: Masonry not initialized.");
      return;
    }
    clearTimeout(reflowTimer);
    reflowTimer = setTimeout(function () {
      console.log("Masonry: Reflow executed!");
      try {
        // ReSharper disable once PossiblyUnassignedProperty
        $('.card--layout').masonry('layout');
      } catch (err) {
        //ignore error, likely masonry is not done loading
      };

    }, 50);
  }

  function forceMasonryReflow(duration, interval) {
    var counter = 0;
    var reflow = setInterval(function () {
      console.log("Masonry: Forcing reflow...");

      try {
        if ($('.card--layout').data('masonry')) {
          // ReSharper disable once PossiblyUnassignedProperty
          $('.card--layout').masonry('layout');
        }
      } catch (err) {
        //ignore error, likely masonry is not done loading
      };

      counter += interval;
      if (counter === duration) {
        clearInterval(reflow);
      }
    }, interval);
  }
  $(document).ready(function () {
    forceMasonryReflow(10000, 1000);
  });
       </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   jQuery.fn.getPath = function () {
    if (this.length != 1) throw 'Requires one element.';

    var path, node = this;
    while (node.length) {
        var realNode = node[0], name = realNode.localName;
        if (!name) break;
        name = name.toLowerCase();

        var parent = node.parent();

        var siblings = parent.children(name);
        if (siblings.length > 1) { 
            name += ':eq(' + siblings.index(realNode) + ')';
        }

        path = name + (path ? '>' + path : '');
        node = parent;
    }

    return path;
};
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function () {
	var wrappers = $(".fancybox-wrapper");
	var idint = 0;
	if ($(wrappers).length < 1) return false; // <-- didn't find any fancy boxes

	$(wrappers).get().forEach(function (wrapperobj) {
		var elepath = $(wrapperobj).getPath();
		var wrapper = $(elepath);
		var idstring = "fancybox" + idint;
		$(wrapper).attr('id', idstring);
		if ($(wrapper).parents(".hidden-print").length > 0)	return false;

		//gather data
		var caption = $(wrapper).find('.thumb-caption-container').first();
		var captext = $(caption).find('.thumb-caption').text();
		//format new html block
		var img = $("#" + idstring).find('img').first();
		var src = $(img).attr("src");
		var newhtml = "<a href='" + src + "' class='fancybox' data-caption='" + captext + "' >" + img[0].outerHTML + caption[0].outerHTML;
		$("#" + idstring).html(newhtml);

		//redefine some data
		var anchor = $("#" + idstring).find('a');

		//init fancybox
		$(anchor).fancybox({
			beforeShow: function () {
				this.title = $(this.element).data("caption");
			}
		});
		idint++;
	});
});
  </script>

   function isInHotJarSection(hotJarSections) {
  var inSection = false;
  hotJarSections.forEach( function(i) { if(window.location.pathname.indexOf(i) > -1) inSection = true; })
  return inSection;
}

hotjarsection = ["/"];

if(hotjarpages.indexOf(window.location.pathname) > -1  || isInHotJarSection(hotjarsection))

	initHealioHotJar();
}

	h._hjSettings={hjid:980112,hjsv:6};

	a=o.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];

	r=o.createElement('script');r.async=1;

	r.src=t+h._hjSettings.hjid+j+h._hjSettings.hjsv;

	a.appendChild(r);

	})(window,document,'https://static.hotjar.com/c/hotjar-','.js?sv=');
}

  <script>
   function addidentitylink() {
	if ($j.cookie != null && $j.cookie('IDL') == null) {
        //if (!window.Visitor.acceptscookies) return;
	    var tag = document.createElement('script');
	    tag.src = 'https://id.rlcdn.com/474046.gif';
	    document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].appendChild(tag);
	    $j.cookie('IDL', '1', { expires: 120, path: '/', domain: '.healio.com' });
	}
}

$j(window).load(function() {
  if (window.Visitor !== undefined) addidentitylink();
  else $j(window).one("globalsloaded", function () { addidentitylink(); });
});

  <script>
   function hasAdblock() {
        var a = document.createElement('div');
        a.innerHTML = '&nbsp;';
        a.className = 'adsbox pub_300x250 pub_300x250m pub_728x90 text-ad textAd text_ad adglare ad-server';
        a.style = 'width: 1px !important; height: 1px !important; position: absolute !important; left: -10000px !important; top: -1000px !important;';
        var r = false;
        try {
            document.body.appendChild(a);
            var e = document.getElementsByClassName('adsbox')[0];
            if(e.offsetHeight === 0 || e.clientHeight === 0) r = true;
            if(window.getComputedStyle !== undefined) {
                var tmp = window.getComputedStyle(e, null);
                if(tmp && (tmp.getPropertyValue('display') == 'none' || tmp.getPropertyValue('visibility') == 'hidden')) r = true;
            }
            document.body.removeChild(a);
        } catch (e) {}
        return r;
    }
